Cargo">Turkish Cargo</a><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> </td><td> <a href="/wiki/Istanbul%E2%80%93Atat%C3%BCrk" class="mw-redirect" title="Istanbul\xe2\x80\x93Atat\xc3\xbcrk">Istanbul\xe2\x80\x93Atat\xc3\xbcrk</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_facilities">Other facilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Other facilities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="CargoCity">CargoCity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: CargoCity">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport is the second-largest <a href="/wiki/Multimodal_transport" title="Multimodal transport">multimodal transport</a> airport in Europe and has several logistics facilities. These facilities are grouped at two areas at the airport ground: In the north (CargoCity Nord) and in the south (CargoCity S\xc3\xbcd). In 2010 it was the second-busiest airport by cargo traffic in Europe after <a href="/wiki/Paris%E2%80%93Charles_de_Gaulle_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Paris\xe2\x80\x93Charles de Gaulle Airport">Paris\xe2\x80\x93Charles de Gaulle Airport</a>, handling 2,231,348 <a href="/wiki/Tonne" title="Tonne">metric tonnes</a> of loaded and unloaded freight.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> CargoCity is the name of the two large main areas featuring most of the airport\'s freight handling facilities:\n</p>\n<ul><li>The 98 hectare large <b>CargoCity S\xc3\xbcd</b> (<i>South</i>) is home to a cargo centre for dispatch service providers and freight forwarding businesses. Several transport companies like <a href="/wiki/DHL_Global_Forwarding" title="DHL Global Forwarding">DHL Global Forwarding</a>, <a href="/wiki/Air_China" title="Air China">Air China</a>, LUG Aircargo Handling (Emirates, Japan Airlines, Korean Air, Cargolux Airlines, Aegean Airlines, Delta Air Lines, Siberian Airlines, South African Airways, Uzbekistan Airways) and Fraport Cargo Services are based here.</li>\n<li><b>CargoCity Nord</b> (<i>North</i>) is the headquarters of <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa_Cargo" title="Lufthansa Cargo">Lufthansa Cargo</a>. Additional facilities here are a Perishables Centre for fresh produced goods and the Frankfurt Animal Lounge for the transport of living animals.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Airport_City">Airport City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Airport City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_FAC_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg/220px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg/330px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg/440px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_FAC_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="966" data-file-height="1288" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_FAC_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Frankfurt Airport Centre 1</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_The_Squaire.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg/220px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg/330px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg/440px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_The_Squaire.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1288" data-file-height="966" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_The_Squaire.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Squaire</div></div></div>\n<p>The airport ground and the surrounding area of Frankfurt Airport offer a large variety of on-airport businesses as well as airport-related businesses, including office space, hotels, shopping areas, conference rooms and car parks. The development of an <a href="/wiki/Airport_city" title="Airport city">airport city</a> has significantly accelerated in recent years.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Frankfurt_Airport_Centres">Frankfurt Airport Centres</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Frankfurt Airport Centres">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The Frankfurt Airport Centre 1 (FAC 1) near Terminal 1 offers office and conference facilities, the newer FAC 2 is located within Terminal 2 and offers office space for airlines.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Airport_City_Mall">Airport City Mall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Airport City Mall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The Airport City Mall is located on the landside of Terminal 1, departure hall B. It offers national and international retailers and label stores, a supermarket and several restaurants.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Squaire">The Squaire</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: The Squaire">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/The_Squaire" title="The Squaire">The Squaire</a></div>\n<p>The Squaire is an office building with a total floor area of 140,000&#160;m<sup>2</sup> (1,506,900&#160;sq&#160;ft). It is directly connected to Terminal 1 through a connecting corridor for pedestrians. The accounting firm <a href="/wiki/KPMG" title="KPMG">KPMG</a>, Lufthansa and two <a href="/wiki/Hilton_Hotels_%26_Resorts" title="Hilton Hotels &amp; Resorts">Hilton Hotels</a> (<i>Hilton Garden Inn Frankfurt Airport</i> <sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> with 334 rooms and <a href="/wiki/Hilton_Frankfurt_Airport" title="Hilton Frankfurt Airport">Hilton Frankfurt Airport</a> with 249 rooms) occupy space in The Squaire.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Main_Airport_Centre">Main Airport Centre</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Main Airport Centre">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>The Main Airport Centre, named after the <a href="/wiki/Main_(river)" title="Main (river)">Main river</a>, is an office building with ten floors and about 51,000&#160;m<sup>2</sup> (549,000&#160;sq&#160;ft) of office space. It is located at the edge of the Frankfurt City Forest near Terminal 2.\n</p>\n<h4><span id="Sheraton_Hotel_.26_Conference_Centre"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sheraton_Hotel_&amp;_Conference_Centre">Sheraton Hotel &amp; Conference Centre</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Sheraton Hotel &amp; Conference Centre">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Sheraton_Hotels_and_Resorts" title="Sheraton Hotels and Resorts">Sheraton Hotels and Resorts</a> offers 1,008 guest rooms adjacent to Terminal 1 and a <a href="/wiki/Conference_centre" class="mw-redirect" title="Conference centre">conference centre</a> for up to 200 delegates.\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gateway_Gardens">Gateway Gardens</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Gateway Gardens">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Gateway Gardens is a former housing area for the US Air Force personnel based at the Rhein-Main Air Base, close to Terminal 2. Like the air base, the housing area was closed in 2005. Since then the area is being developed into a business location for airport-related companies. Lufthansa moved its <a href="/wiki/Airline_meal" title="Airline meal">airline catering</a> subsidiary <a href="/wiki/LSG_Sky_Chefs" class="mw-redirect" title="LSG Sky Chefs">LSG Sky Chefs</a> to Gateway Gardens, Condor and <a href="/wiki/SunExpress" title="SunExpress">SunExpress</a> are headquartered here. <a href="/wiki/DB_Schenker" title="DB Schenker">DB Schenker</a>, the logistics company of <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Bahn" title="Deutsche Bahn">Deutsche Bahn</a>, have built a 66&#160;m (217&#160;ft) high-rise building.\n</p><p>In December 2019, local trains were re-routed to run via <a href="/wiki/Gateway_Gardens_station" title="Gateway Gardens station">Gateway Gardens station</a>. The new stop for <a href="/wiki/S-Train" class="mw-redirect" title="S-Train">S-Bahn</a> trains is located between <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Airport_regional_station" title="Frankfurt Airport regional station">Frankfurt Airport Regional Station</a> and <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Stadion_station" title="Frankfurt Stadion station">Frankfurt-Stadion station</a>. The journey time will increase by 4 minutes but Deutsche Bahn have stated that they will use new trains (ET423) which will be faster and have more capacity.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Further_users">Further users</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Further users">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg/220px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg/330px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg/440px-Frankfurt_Flughafen%2C_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1288" data-file-height="966" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurt_Flughafen,_Lufthansa_Aviation_Center.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Lufthansa Aviation Centre</div></div></div>\n<ul><li>Fraport\'s facilities are on the property of Frankfurt Airport.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> Its head office building is by Gate 3.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> The newly constructed<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> headquarters were inaugurated there in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The Fraport Driving School (Fraport Fahrschule) is in Building 501 of CargoCity South (CargoCity S\xc3\xbcd).<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Lufthansa\'s main building, where the board of directors is seated, is called Lufthansa Aviation Centre (LAC).<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Lufthansa operates the Lufthansa Aviation Center (LAC), Building 366 at Frankfurt Airport.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Several company departments, including Corporate Communications,<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> Investor Relations,<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> and Media Relations,<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> are based at the LAC. Lufthansa also uses several other buildings in the area, including the <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa_Flight_Training" class="mw-redirect" title="Lufthansa Flight Training">Lufthansa Flight Training Center</a> for <a href="/wiki/Flight_training" title="Flight training">flight training</a> operations and the <i>Lufthansa Basis BG2</i><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> as a central base and for crew briefing. As of 2011 <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa_Cargo" title="Lufthansa Cargo">Lufthansa Cargo</a> has been headquartered in Building 451 of the Frankfurt Airport area.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> As of 2012 Lufthansa Cargo is located at Gate 25 in the CargoCity Nord area, <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa_Technik" title="Lufthansa Technik">Lufthansa Technik</a> is located at Gate 23 and in the CargoCity S\xc3\xbcd area.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Star Alliance, an airline alliance, has its headquarters at the Frankfurt Airport Centre 1 (FAC 1) adjacent to Terminal 1.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Airmail Centre Frankfurt, a joint venture of Lufthansa Cargo, Fraport, and <a href="/wiki/Deutsche_Post" title="Deutsche Post">Deutsche Post</a> for <a href="/wiki/Airmail" title="Airmail">airmail</a> transport, has its head office in Building 189, between Terminals 1 and 2.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Aero_Lloyd" title="Aero Lloyd">Aero Lloyd</a> previously had its head office in Building 182.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Statistics">Statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Annual_traffic">Annual traffic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Annual traffic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<style href="/wiki/Lufthansa" title="Lufthansa">Lufthansa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Singapore_Airlines" title="Singapore Airlines">Singapore Airlines</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ground_transport">Ground transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Ground transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport can easily be accessed by car, taxi, train or bus as it features an extensive transport network. There are two railway stations at the airport: one for suburban/regional trains and one for long-distance trains.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rail">Rail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Rail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Regional_station">Regional station</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Regional station">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurter_(Main)_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg/220px-Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg/330px-Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg/440px-Frankfurter_%28Main%29_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4224" data-file-height="3168" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Frankfurter_(Main)_Flughafen_Regionalbahnhof-_auf_Bahnsteig_zu_Gleis_3-_S-Bahn_Rhein-Main_420_227-8_18.10.2009.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>S-Bahn at the regional station</div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Airport_regional_station" title="Frankfurt Airport regional station">Frankfurt Airport regional station</a></div>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport regional station (<i>Frankfurt Flughafen Regionalbahnhof</i>) at Terminal 1, concourse B, provides access to the S-Bahn commuter rail lines <i>S8</i> and <i>S9</i>. Each of these lines have trains departing every 15 minutes during daytime to <a href="/wiki/Hanau_Hauptbahnhof" title="Hanau Hauptbahnhof">Hanau Central Station</a> eastwards via <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Central_Station" class="mw-redirect" title="Frankfurt Central Station">Frankfurt Central Station</a> and <a href="/wiki/Offenbach_(Main)_Ost_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Offenbach (Main) Ost station">Offenbach East Station</a> or <a href="/wiki/Wiesbaden_Hauptbahnhof" title="Wiesbaden Hauptbahnhof">Wiesbaden Central Station</a> westwards via <a href="/wiki/R%C3%BCsselsheim_station" title="R\xc3\xbcsselsheim station">R\xc3\xbcsselsheim</a> or <a href="/wiki/Mainz_Hauptbahnhof" title="Mainz Hauptbahnhof">Mainz Central Station</a> (line S8) or <a href="/wiki/Mainz-Kastel_station" title="Mainz-Kastel station">Mainz-Kastel Station</a> (line S9).\n</p><p>The journey time to Frankfurt Central Station is 10\xe2\x80\x9312 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-trains_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-trains-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Regional-Express" title="Regional-Express">Regional Express (RE)</a> trains to <a href="/wiki/Saarbr%C3%BCcken_Hauptbahnhof" title="Saarbr\xc3\xbccken Hauptbahnhof">Saarbr\xc3\xbccken</a>, <a href="/wiki/Koblenz_Hauptbahnhof" title="Koblenz Hauptbahnhof">Koblenz</a> or <a href="/wiki/W%C3%BCrzburg_Hauptbahnhof" title="W\xc3\xbcrzburg Hauptbahnhof">W\xc3\xbcrzburg</a> call at this station. These trains provide less frequent but additional connections between Frankfurt Airport and the Central Station.<sup id="cite_ref-trains_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-trains-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Long-distance_station">Long-distance station</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Long-distance station">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG/220px-Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG/330px-Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG/440px-Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2816" data-file-height="2112" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Flughafen-Fernbahnsteig-Frankfurt_am_Main.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Platforms at the long-distance station</div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Airport_long-distance_station" title="Frankfurt Airport long-distance station">Frankfurt Airport long-distance station</a></div>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport long-distance station (<i>Frankfurt Flughafen Fernbahnhof</i>) was opened in 1999. The station is squeezed in between the <a href="/wiki/Bundesautobahn_3" title="Bundesautobahn 3">motorway A 3</a> and the four-lane <i>Bundesstra\xc3\x9fe</i> B43, linked to Terminal 1 by a connecting corridor for pedestrians that bridges the Autobahn. It is the end point of the newly built <a href="/wiki/Cologne%E2%80%93Frankfurt_high-speed_rail_line" title="Cologne\xe2\x80\x93Frankfurt high-speed rail line">Cologne\xe2\x80\x93Frankfurt high-speed rail line</a>, which links southern Germany to the <a href="/wiki/Rhine-Ruhr" title="Rhine-Ruhr">Rhine-Ruhr</a> metropolitan area, the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> via <a href="/wiki/Cologne" title="Cologne">Cologne</a> at speeds up to 300&#160;km/h (190&#160;mph). About 10 trains per hour depart in all directions.<sup id="cite_ref-trains_106-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-trains-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Deutsche Bahn operates the <a href="/wiki/AIRail_Service" title="AIRail Service">AIRail Service</a> in conjunction with Lufthansa, American Airlines and Emirates. The service operates to the central stations of <a href="/wiki/Bonn_Hauptbahnhof" title="Bonn Hauptbahnhof">Bonn</a>, <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ln_Hauptbahnhof" title="K\xc3\xb6ln Hauptbahnhof">Cologne</a>, <a href="/wiki/D%C3%BCsseldorf_Hauptbahnhof" title="D\xc3\xbcsseldorf Hauptbahnhof">D\xc3\xbcsseldorf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Freiburg_Hauptbahnhof" title="Freiburg Hauptbahnhof">Freiburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Karlsruhe_Hauptbahnhof" title="Karlsruhe Hauptbahnhof">Karlsruhe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Leipzig_Hauptbahnhof" title="Leipzig Hauptbahnhof">Leipzig</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hamburg_Hauptbahnhof" title="Hamburg Hauptbahnhof">Hamburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hannover_Hauptbahnhof" title="Hannover Hauptbahnhof">Hannover</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mannheim_Hauptbahnhof" title="Mannheim Hauptbahnhof">Mannheim</a>, <a href="/wiki/M%C3%BCnchen_Hauptbahnhof" title="M\xc3\xbcnchen Hauptbahnhof">Munich</a>, <a href="/wiki/N%C3%BCrnberg_Hauptbahnhof" title="N\xc3\xbcrnberg Hauptbahnhof">Nuremberg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stuttgart_Hauptbahnhof" title="Stuttgart Hauptbahnhof">Stuttgart</a> and to <a href="/wiki/Kassel-Wilhelmsh%C3%B6he_station" title="Kassel-Wilhelmsh\xc3\xb6he station">Kassel-Wilhelmsh\xc3\xb6he</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Car">Car</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Car">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport is located in the Frankfurt City Forest and directly connected to an Autobahn intersection called <a href="/wiki/Frankfurter_Kreuz" title="Frankfurter Kreuz">Frankfurter Kreuz</a> where the A3 and A5 meet. It takes a 10\xe2\x80\x9315 minutes by car or taxi to get to Frankfurt Central Station or the centre of the city.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Passengers driving their own cars can park in multilevel parking garages (mostly underground) along the terminals. A long term holiday parking lot is located south of the runways and connected by shuttle bus to the terminals.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bicycle">Bicycle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Bicycle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Terminal 1 and Terminal 2 can be reached by bicycle because one of the roads that run north of the airport passing the terminals can legally be used by bicycle. The airport authority has confirmed that the newly built terminal 3 will also be reachable by bicycle.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bus_and_coaches">Bus and coaches</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Bus and coaches">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Various transport companies provide bus services to the airport from the surrounding areas as well as by coach to long-distance destinations.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Previously <a href="/wiki/All_Nippon_Airways" title="All Nippon Airways">All Nippon Airways</a> operated a bus service to D\xc3\xbcsseldorf exclusively for ANA customers; that way D\xc3\xbcsseldorf passengers would be transported to Frankfurt Airport to board their ANA flights.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> In 2014 ANA established a separate flight from Tokyo to D\xc3\xbcsseldorf,<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> causing the bus services to end.<sup id="cite_ref-ANApress_112-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ANApress-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ground_transport_statistics">Ground transport statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Ground transport statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 2006, 29.5% of the 12,299,192 passengers whose air travel originated in Frankfurt came by private car, 27.9% came by rail, 20.4% by taxi, 11.1% parked their car at the airport for the duration of their trip, 5.3% came by bus, and 4.6% arrived with a rental car.<sup id="cite_ref-Fraport_MVG-MF_2007_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fraport_MVG-MF_2007-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Incidents_and_accidents">Incidents and accidents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Incidents and accidents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li>On 22 May 1983, during an <a href="/wiki/Air_show" title="Air show">air show</a> at Rhein-Main Air Base, a Canadian <a href="/wiki/Royal_Canadian_Air_Force" title="Royal Canadian Air Force">RCAF</a> <a href="/wiki/Lockheed_F-104_Starfighter" title="Lockheed F-104 Starfighter">Lockheed F-104 Starfighter</a> crashed into a nearby road, hitting a car and killing all passengers, a vicar\'s family of five. The pilot was able to <a href="/wiki/Ejection_seat" title="Ejection seat">eject</a>.</li>\n<li>On 19 June 1985, <a href="/wiki/1985_Frankfurt_airport_bombing" title="1985 Frankfurt airport bombing">a bomb cloaked in a canvas bag was detonated</a> approx at 14:42 in the afternoon in Hall B of the Rhein Main Frankfurt Airport, decimating that section of the airport. The blast resulted in 3 deaths and 32 injuries, of which 4 were considered serious.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>In September 2007, German authorities arrested <a href="/wiki/2007_bomb_plot_in_Germany" title="2007 bomb plot in Germany">three suspected</a> terrorists for plotting a "massive" terror attack, which posed "an imminent threat" to Frankfurt Airport and the US Air Force base in <a href="/wiki/Ramstein_Air_Base" title="Ramstein Air Base">Ramstein</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>On 2 March 2011, <a href="/wiki/2011_Frankfurt_Airport_shooting" title="2011 Frankfurt Airport shooting">a gunman opened fire</a> on a bus carrying US Air Force personnel at Frankfurt Airport, killing two and wounding two others.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_media">In media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Frankfurt_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: In media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Frankfurt Airport is featured in the <a href="/wiki/Discovery_Channel_(UK_and_Ireland)" class="mw-redirect" title="Discovery Channel (UK and Ireland)">Discovery Channel</a> series <i><a href="/wiki/X-Ray_Mega_Airport" title="X-Ray Mega Airport">X-Ray Mega Airport</a></i> (also known as <i>Inside Frankfurt Airport</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Jinder_Mahal" title="Jinder Mahal">Jinder Mahal</a> pinned <a href="/wiki/R-Truth" title="R-Truth">R-Truth</a> at the Frankfurt Airport for the 24/7 Championship. This title change was shown on WWE.com and WWE\'s official social media accounts.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span
